<script type="text/javascript">

if (!window.cwc) {
  window.cwc = {};
}

cwc.antiCSRFEnabled = true;
cwc.csrfSimpleURLs = 'service.do, detail.do, list.do, mashup.do, frames.do, printList.do, printDetail.do, uim.do, nav.menu, wf, ce, cm, /upload, /imageupload, /attachmentupload, /uniqueupload'.split(",");
cwc.csrfPatterns = 'attachments/, /download/, /api/smc/, api/report/, /branding/configuration, /branding/imageupload, /api/calendar'.split(",");
cwc.csrfTokenName = 'aftk-1207';
cwc.csrfTokenValue = '-1264689741';
cwc.detailAction = 'detail.do';
cwc.listAction = 'list.do';

cwc.getCSRFTokenName = function() {
  return cwc.csrfTokenName;
};

cwc.getCSRFTokenValue = function() {
  return cwc.csrfTokenValue;
};

/**
 * Convert a URL to be CSRF safe
 * @param originUrl The given URL to convert
 * @param isCSRFEnabledFree, Optional parameter, Default is false. If true, convert anyway without checking
 *        antiCSRFEnabled parameter value, or else the conversion will only occur when antiCSRFEnabled is true.
 * @param isQueryHashFree, Optional parameter, Default is false. If true, a query hash free parameter will be added to
 * the url
 * @returns A CSRF safe URL if conversion is required, otherwise returns the original URL.
 */
cwc.toCSRFSafe = function(originUrl, isCSRFEnabledFree, isQueryHashFree) {
  if (hpsm.StringUtils.isEmpty(originUrl)) {
    return originUrl;
  }
  if (originUrl.indexOf(cwc.getCSRFTokenName()) == -1) {
    if (cwc.isCSRFValidationRequired(originUrl, isCSRFEnabledFree)) {
      var builder = new hpsm.URLBuilder();
          builder.setPath(originUrl);
          builder.setCSRFToken(cwc.getCSRFTokenName(), cwc.getCSRFTokenValue());
          return builder.toURL(isCSRFEnabledFree, isQueryHashFree);
    }
  } else {
    // Uncomment this if debugging.
    /*if (cwc.jsDebug == true) {
      cwc.logMessage("debug", "cwc-base.js", "The URL which already contains CSRF token is duplicately calling cwc.toCSRFSafe(url): " + originUrl);
    }*/
  }
  return originUrl;
};

cwc.isCSRFValidationRequired = function(targetUrl, isCSRFEnabledFree) {
  if (!(cwc.antiCSRFEnabled || !!isCSRFEnabledFree)) {
    return false;
  }
  for (var i=0, len=cwc.csrfSimpleURLs.length; i<len; ++i) {
    var action = cwc.csrfSimpleURLs[i].trim();
    if (cwc.isSimpleUrlMatched(targetUrl, action)) {
      return true;
    }
  }
  for (var i=0, len=cwc.csrfPatterns.length; i<len; ++i) {
    var pattern = cwc.csrfPatterns[i].trim();
    if (cwc.isPatternMatched(targetUrl, pattern)) {
      return true;
    }
  }
  return false;
};

cwc.isSimpleUrlMatched = function(targetUrl, action) {
  if (hpsm.StringUtils.isEmpty(targetUrl) || hpsm.StringUtils.isEmpty(action)) {
    return false;
  }
  var inx = targetUrl.indexOf('?');
  if (inx >= 0) {
    targetUrl = targetUrl.substring(0, inx);
  }
  if (targetUrl.indexOf('/') >= 0 && action.charAt(0) != '/') {
    action = '/' + action;
  }
  inx = targetUrl.indexOf(action);
  return inx >= 0 && inx == targetUrl.length - action.length;
};

cwc.isPatternMatched = function(targetUrl, pattern) {
  if (hpsm.StringUtils.isEmpty(targetUrl) || hpsm.StringUtils.isEmpty(pattern)) {
    return false;
  }
  var regex = new RegExp(pattern);
  return regex.test(targetUrl);
};

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    function refreshTemplate(){
        var s = document.createElement("script");
        s.src = 'refreshTemplate.jsp';
        document.body.appendChild(s);
        setTimeout(function(){
            document.body.removeChild(s)
        }, 5000);
    }

    function toggleCompactMode(){
      var s = document.createElement("script");
      s.src = 'toggleCompact.jsp';
      document.body.appendChild(s);
      var toggleButton = document.getElementById("toggleMode");
      toggleButton.innerHTML = toggleButton.innerHTML == "Compact" ? "Normal" : "Compact";

      setTimeout(function(){
        document.body.removeChild(s);
        window.location.reload(true);
      }, 5000);
    }

    function turnVertical() {
      if (cwc.isHorizontalLayout()) {
        var vBtn = Ext.get('v-layout'), hBtn = Ext.get('h-layout');
        var tab = cwc.getActiveTab();
        vBtn.addClass('active');
        hBtn.removeClass('active');
        if(tab.hasListDetail()) {
            var win = tab.getFrameWindow();
            if (win && win.cwc && win.cwc.ListDetailController) {
              win.cwc.ListDetailController.verticalLayout();
            }
        }else {
            cwc.setListDetailOriental(cwc.ORIENTAL_VERTICAL);
        }
      }
    }

    function turnHorizontal() {
      if (cwc.isVerticalLayout()) {
        var vBtn = Ext.get('v-layout'), hBtn = Ext.get('h-layout');
        var tab = cwc.getActiveTab();
        vBtn.removeClass('active');
        hBtn.addClass('active');
        if(tab.hasListDetail()) {
            var win = tab.getFrameWindow();
            if (win && win.cwc && win.cwc.ListDetailController) {
              win.cwc.ListDetailController.horizontalLayout();
            }
        }else {
            cwc.setListDetailOriental(cwc.ORIENTAL_HORIZONTAL);
        }
      }
    }

    Ext.onReady(function(){
      //Move cwc tool buttons in the head
      var toolbar = new cwc.ux.Toolbar();

      if('1'==0)
      {
        var vBtn = new Ext.Button({
          id: 'v-layout',
          xtype: 'button',
          qtip: top.cwc.VERTICAL,
          iconCls: 'icon-vertical',
          handler: function () {
            turnVertical();
          },
          listeners: {
            afterrender: function(btn) {
              if(cwc.isVerticalLayout()) {
                this.el.addClass('active');
              }
              this.btnEl.set({tabindex: -1});
              this.setText(top.cwc.VERTICAL);
            }
          }
        });
        var hBtn =  new Ext.Button({
          id: 'h-layout',
          xtype: 'button',
          qtip: top.cwc.HORIZONTAL,
          iconCls: 'icon-horizontal',
          handler: function () {
            turnHorizontal();
          },
          listeners: {
            afterrender: function(btn) {
              // Fix the image position issue in FF and IE
              if(Ext.isGecko) {
                this.el.setStyle('background-position', '-29px 3px');
              } else if (Ext.isIE) {
                this.el.setStyle('background-position', '-26px 3px');
              }
              if(!cwc.isVerticalLayout()) {
                this.el.addClass('active');
              }
              this.btnEl.set({tabindex: -1});
              this.setText(top.cwc.HORIZONTAL);
            }
          }
        });
        toolbar.addComponents([
          vBtn, hBtn
        ], true);
        toolbar.render(Ext.get('layout-switch'));
      }

      if (false) {

    });

<script type="text/javascript">

if (!window.cwc) {
  window.cwc = {};
}

cwc.antiCSRFEnabled = true;
cwc.csrfSimpleURLs = 'service.do, detail.do, list.do, mashup.do, frames.do, printList.do, printDetail.do, uim.do, nav.menu, wf, ce, cm, /upload, /imageupload, /attachmentupload, /uniqueupload'.split(",");
cwc.csrfPatterns = 'attachments/, /download/, /api/smc/, api/report/, /branding/configuration, /branding/imageupload, /api/calendar'.split(",");
cwc.csrfTokenName = 'aftk-19';
cwc.csrfTokenValue = '-19638500';
cwc.detailAction = 'detail.do';
cwc.listAction = 'list.do';

cwc.getCSRFTokenName = function() {
  return cwc.csrfTokenName;
};

cwc.getCSRFTokenValue = function() {
  return cwc.csrfTokenValue;
};

/**
 * Convert a URL to be CSRF safe
 * @param originUrl The given URL to convert
 * @param isCSRFEnabledFree, Optional parameter, Default is false. If true, convert anyway without checking
 *        antiCSRFEnabled parameter value, or else the conversion will only occur when antiCSRFEnabled is true.
 * @param isQueryHashFree, Optional parameter, Default is false. If true, a query hash free parameter will be added to
 * the url
 * @returns A CSRF safe URL if conversion is required, otherwise returns the original URL.
 */
cwc.toCSRFSafe = function(originUrl, isCSRFEnabledFree, isQueryHashFree) {
  if (hpsm.StringUtils.isEmpty(originUrl)) {
    return originUrl;
  }
  if (originUrl.indexOf(cwc.getCSRFTokenName()) == -1) {
    if (cwc.isCSRFValidationRequired(originUrl, isCSRFEnabledFree)) {
      var builder = new hpsm.URLBuilder();
          builder.setPath(originUrl);
          builder.setCSRFToken(cwc.getCSRFTokenName(), cwc.getCSRFTokenValue());
          return builder.toURL(isCSRFEnabledFree, isQueryHashFree);
    }
  } else {
    // Uncomment this if debugging.
    /*if (cwc.jsDebug == true) {
      cwc.logMessage("debug", "cwc-base.js", "The URL which already contains CSRF token is duplicately calling cwc.toCSRFSafe(url): " + originUrl);
    }*/
  }
  return originUrl;
};

cwc.isCSRFValidationRequired = function(targetUrl, isCSRFEnabledFree) {
  if (!(cwc.antiCSRFEnabled || !!isCSRFEnabledFree)) {
    return false;
  }
  for (var i=0, len=cwc.csrfSimpleURLs.length; i<len; ++i) {
    var action = cwc.csrfSimpleURLs[i].trim();
    if (cwc.isSimpleUrlMatched(targetUrl, action)) {
      return true;
    }
  }
  for (var i=0, len=cwc.csrfPatterns.length; i<len; ++i) {
    var pattern = cwc.csrfPatterns[i].trim();
    if (cwc.isPatternMatched(targetUrl, pattern)) {
      return true;
    }
  }
  return false;
};

cwc.isSimpleUrlMatched = function(targetUrl, action) {
  if (hpsm.StringUtils.isEmpty(targetUrl) || hpsm.StringUtils.isEmpty(action)) {
    return false;
  }
  var inx = targetUrl.indexOf('?');
  if (inx >= 0) {
    targetUrl = targetUrl.substring(0, inx);
  }
  if (targetUrl.indexOf('/') >= 0 && action.charAt(0) != '/') {
    action = '/' + action;
  }
  inx = targetUrl.indexOf(action);
  return inx >= 0 && inx == targetUrl.length - action.length;
};

cwc.isPatternMatched = function(targetUrl, pattern) {
  if (hpsm.StringUtils.isEmpty(targetUrl) || hpsm.StringUtils.isEmpty(pattern)) {
    return false;
  }
  var regex = new RegExp(pattern);
  return regex.test(targetUrl);
};

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    function refreshTemplate(){
        var s = document.createElement("script");
        s.src = 'refreshTemplate.jsp';
        document.body.appendChild(s);
        setTimeout(function(){
            document.body.removeChild(s)
        }, 5000);
    }

    function toggleCompactMode(){
      var s = document.createElement("script");
      s.src = 'toggleCompact.jsp';
      document.body.appendChild(s);
      var toggleButton = document.getElementById("toggleMode");
      toggleButton.innerHTML = toggleButton.innerHTML == "Compact" ? "Normal" : "Compact";

      setTimeout(function(){
        document.body.removeChild(s);
        window.location.reload(true);
      }, 5000);
    }

    function turnVertical() {
      if (cwc.isHorizontalLayout()) {
        var vBtn = Ext.get('v-layout'), hBtn = Ext.get('h-layout');
        var tab = cwc.getActiveTab();
        vBtn.addClass('active');
        hBtn.removeClass('active');
        if(tab.hasListDetail()) {
            var win = tab.getFrameWindow();
            if (win && win.cwc && win.cwc.ListDetailController) {
              win.cwc.ListDetailController.verticalLayout();
            }
        }else {
            cwc.setListDetailOriental(cwc.ORIENTAL_VERTICAL);
        }
      }
    }

    function turnHorizontal() {
      if (cwc.isVerticalLayout()) {
        var vBtn = Ext.get('v-layout'), hBtn = Ext.get('h-layout');
        var tab = cwc.getActiveTab();
        vBtn.removeClass('active');
        hBtn.addClass('active');
        if(tab.hasListDetail()) {
            var win = tab.getFrameWindow();
            if (win && win.cwc && win.cwc.ListDetailController) {
              win.cwc.ListDetailController.horizontalLayout();
            }
        }else {
            cwc.setListDetailOriental(cwc.ORIENTAL_HORIZONTAL);
        }
      }
    }

    Ext.onReady(function(){
      //Move cwc tool buttons in the head
      var toolbar = new cwc.ux.Toolbar();

      if('1'==0)
      {
        var vBtn = new Ext.Button({
          id: 'v-layout',
          xtype: 'button',
          qtip: top.cwc.VERTICAL,
          iconCls: 'icon-vertical',
          handler: function () {
            turnVertical();
          },
          listeners: {
            afterrender: function(btn) {
              if(cwc.isVerticalLayout()) {
                this.el.addClass('active');
              }
              this.btnEl.set({tabindex: -1});
              this.setText(top.cwc.VERTICAL);
            }
          }
        });
        var hBtn =  new Ext.Button({
          id: 'h-layout',
          xtype: 'button',
          qtip: top.cwc.HORIZONTAL,
          iconCls: 'icon-horizontal',
          handler: function () {
            turnHorizontal();
          },
          listeners: {
            afterrender: function(btn) {
              // Fix the image position issue in FF and IE
              if(Ext.isGecko) {
                this.el.setStyle('background-position', '-29px 3px');
              } else if (Ext.isIE) {
                this.el.setStyle('background-position', '-26px 3px');
              }
              if(!cwc.isVerticalLayout()) {
                this.el.addClass('active');
              }
              this.btnEl.set({tabindex: -1});
              this.setText(top.cwc.HORIZONTAL);
            }
          }
        });
        toolbar.addComponents([
          vBtn, hBtn
        ], true);
        toolbar.render(Ext.get('layout-switch'));
      }

      if (false) {
        toolbar = new cwc.ux.Toolbar();
        toolbar.addComponents([{
            "xtype":"cmdLineInput",
            "isUniSearchActive":'0',
            "isCmdActive":'0',
            "width":90,
            "url":"detail.do?thread=0",
            "valueParamName":"commandLine",
            "commandBtn":{
                "lineField":cwc.COMMAND_LINE_FIELD,
                "tooltip":cwc.COMMAND_LINE_BTN
            },
            "uniSearchBtn":{
                "lineField":"Search",
                "tooltip":"Search"
            }
        }], true);
        toolbar.render(Ext.get('head-button-command'));
      }
      
        toolbar = new cwc.ux.Toolbar();
        var headerBtns =   [];
        if(!window.isEssUser && cwc.smcEnabled) {
          var endUserChatEnabled = cwc.smcModuleConfig.endUserChatEnabled;
          if (endUserChatEnabled) {
            headerBtns.unshift({
              xtype: 'chatRequest',
              hidden: true
            });
          }
          hpsmc.DataLoader.getUserInfo('g571602', this, function (userInfo) {
            var agms = userInfo['assignment'];
            if (agms && agms.length > 0) {
              var chatRequestButtonCmp = Ext.getCmp('smcChatRequestButtonId');
              if (chatRequestButtonCmp) {
                chatRequestButtonCmp.setVisible(true);
                chatRequestButtonCmp.deferAnchorCounter();
              }
              var notificationButtonCmp = Ext.getCmp('smcNotificationButtonId');
              notificationButtonCmp.deferAnchorCounter();
              var alertButtonCmp = Ext.getCmp('topAlertButtonId');
              if(alertButtonCmp) {
                alertButtonCmp.deferAnchorCounter();
              }
            }
          });

          headerBtns.unshift({
            xtype: 'notification'
          });
        }
        if(cwc.todoAlertEnabled){
            headerBtns.unshift({
                xtype: 'topalert'
            });
        }
        if(!cwc.isAccessibleMode && headerBtns.length > 0){
          toolbar.addComponents(['-'], true);
        }
        toolbar.addComponents([{
          xtype: 'cwcMastHeadButtons',
          buttons: headerBtns
        },'-']);
        toolbar.render(Ext.get('head-button-messagehelp'));

      toolbar = new cwc.ux.Toolbar();
      var headerBtns = [{
        xtype: 'messages'
      }];
      if(!window.isEssUser){
        headerBtns.push({
          xtype: 'help'
        });
      }
      toolbar.addComponents([{
        xtype: 'cwcMastHeadButtons',
        buttons: headerBtns
      }, '-']);
      toolbar.render(Ext.get('search-help-userinfo'));

      toolbar = new cwc.ux.Toolbar();
      var headerBtns = [];
      if(cwc.smcSupported){
        headerBtns.push({
          xtype: 'userinfo'
        });
        Ext.get('masthead-user-name-cnt').setStyle('display', 'none');
        Ext.get('user-name-seperator').setStyle('display', 'none');
        Ext.get('logoutlink').setStyle('display', 'none');
      }
      toolbar.addComponents([{
        xtype: 'cwcMastHeadButtons',
        buttons: headerBtns
      }]);
      toolbar.render(Ext.get('user-avatar-info'));

        var smcConfig = cwc.smcModuleConfig;
        if(!isEssUser && smcConfig && cwc.smcEnabled){
          if(!smcConfig.supportList) {
            Ext.Ajax.request({
              method: 'GET',
              url: hpsmc.Utils.toServiceLink('/smcconfig/supportlist'),
              success: function(resp){
                smcConfig.supportList = Ext.decode(resp.responseText);
              },
              failure: function(){
                window.console && console.log("failed to get support list!");
              }
            });
          }
          hpsmc.DataLoader.loadInactivityTimerConfig.defer(5000, hpsmc.DataLoader);
          hpsmc.xmpp.init(smcConfig.domainName, smcConfig.boshURL, smcConfig.pluginURL, smcConfig.maxParticipants);
          hpsmc.xmpp.connect('g571602','g571602', '');
        }
    });
</script>




<script>
Ext.onReady(function() {
  var ux = Ext.namespace('hpsm.ux');
  var stateConfig = {
    isPowerMode : true,
    isCommandSearchStyle : true,
    isCmdActive : false,
    isUniSearchActive: false,
    isSaEnabled: false,
    searchEl : 'gs-input',
    cmdEl : 'cmd-input',
    legacySearchEl : 'gs-trigger',
  };
  ux.initialize(stateConfig);
  cwc.util.setToolbarARIA({'toolbar': Ext.get('cwc_masthead_toolbar')});
});
</script>
